<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>From an early XVIIIth cent. french manuscript. A few pieces (<i>Gavotte, Rondeau, Sonate, La Piémontaise</i>) are intended for harpsichord most probably.
</p>
